        function cdnfallback() {
            if (window.appInsights) {
                var region = "UK South";
                var siteName = "acom-prod-uksouth-02";
                var error = new Error('Bundle - client side cdn fallback to local cdn, region: ' + region + ' , sitename: ' + siteName);

                window.appInsights.trackException({ exception: error });
            }

            if (window.location.search.indexOf('cdn=disable') === -1) {
                window.location.href = '?cdn=disable';
            }
        }

  <script>

    $(window).on('load', function () {
        function enableSSO() {
            setTimeout(function () {
                window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
                var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                iframe.src = '/auth/sso/';
                iframe.setAttribute('id', 'sso-frame');
                iframe.setAttribute('style', 'width: 0; height: 0; border: 0; border: none; position: absolute;');
                iframe.setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
                $('body').prepend(iframe);
            }, 500);
        }

        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin !== 'https://azure.microsoft.com' || event.data !== 'sso-success') {
            return;
            }

            
            window.setTimeout(function () { document.getElementById('sso-frame').contentWindow.location.replace('/auth/sso/'); }, 30 * 60 * 1000);

            
            var enabledSubmitInputs = $('input:enabled[type="submit"], button:enabled[type="submit"]');
            enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', true);

            window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.success')); 

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/sso/info/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    if (data) {
                        $('.auth-container').html(data);
                    }
                })
                .fail(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });

            
            $.ajax({ url: '/auth/antiforgerytoken/', timeout: 3000 })
                .done(function (data) {
                    $('input[name="__RequestVerificationToken"]').replaceWith(data);
                    window.dispatchEvent(createNewEvent('sso.requestVerificationTokenReceived'));
                })
                .always(function () {
                    
                    enabledSubmitInputs.attr('disabled', false);
                });
        }

        
        function createNewEvent(eventName) {
            var event;

            if (typeof (Event) === 'function') {
                event = new Event(eventName);
            } else {
                event = document.createEvent('Event'); 
                event.initEvent(eventName, true, true);
            }

            return event;
        }

        // We won't process requests made from any status page
        if (window.location.pathname.indexOf('/status/') === -1)
        {
            // enable sso only if the userAgent is not safari
            if (!/^((?!chrome|android).)*safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                enableSSO();
            }
        }
    });

</script>

   <section class="section" aria-label="Simplify your workflows and increase efficiency using Azure Machine Learning." data-module="content-image-02"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column large-push-4 large-offset-1 medium-7 medium-push-5"> 
      <img alt="" src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/machine-learning/mlgif-compressed.gif?637585607207708374"> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column large-4 large-pull-8 medium-5 medium-pull-7"> 
      <h2>Boost productivity with machine learning for all skill levels</h2> 
      <p>Rapidly build and deploy machine learning models using tools that meet your needs regardless of skill level. Use built-in Jupyter Notebooks with IntelliSense or the drag-and-drop <a href="/en-us/services/machine-learning/designer/">designer</a>. Accelerate model creation with <a href="/en-us/services/machine-learning/automatedml/">automated machine learning</a>, and access powerful feature engineering, algorithm selection, and hyperparameter-sweeping capabilities. Increase team efficiency with shared datasets, notebooks, models, and customizable dashboards that track all aspects of the machine learning process.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row row-size8"> 
     <div class="column medium-7"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/machine-learning/value-prop-2.png" class="device-wrapper" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-5 large-4 large-offset-1"> 
      <h2>Operationalize at scale with MLOps</h2> 
      <p>Take advantage of <a href="/en-us/services/machine-learning/mlops/">MLOps</a> to streamline the machine learning lifecycle, from building models to deployment and management. Create reproducible workflows with machine learning pipelines, and train, validate, and deploy thousands of models at scale, from the cloud to the edge. Use managed online and batch endpoints to seamlessly deploy and score models without managing the underlying infrastructure. Use Azure DevOps or GitHub Actions to schedule, manage, and automate the machine learning pipelines, and use advanced data-drift analysis to improve model performance over time.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row row-size8"> 
     <div class="column large-push-4 large-offset-1 medium-7 medium-push-5"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/machine-learning/value-prop-3.png" class="device-wrapper" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column large-4 large-pull-8 medium-5 medium-pull-7"> 
      <h2>Build responsible machine learning solutions</h2> 
      <p>Access state-of-the-art <a href="/en-us/services/machine-learning/responsibleML/">responsible machine learning</a> capabilities to understand, control, and help protect your data, models, and processes. Explain model behavior during training and inferencing, and build for fairness by detecting and mitigating model bias. Preserve data privacy throughout the machine learning lifecycle with differential privacy techniques and use confidential computing to secure machine learning assets. Automatically maintain audit trails, track lineage, and use model datasheets to enable accountability.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row row-size8"> 
     <div class="column medium-7"> 
      <img src="//azurecomcdn.azureedge.net/cvt-526390d16d87de1877250c5808f92a928069f41676f250913969acdedd7e9a4a/images/page/services/machine-learning/value-prop-4.png" alt=""> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-5 large-4 large-offset-1"> 
      <h2>Innovate on an open and flexible platform</h2> 
      <p>Get built-in support for open-source tools and frameworks for machine learning model training and inferencing. Use familiar frameworks like PyTorch, TensorFlow, or scikit-learn, or the open and interoperable ONNX format. Choose the development tools that best meet your needs, including popular IDEs, Visual Studio Code, Jupyter Notebooks, and CLIs, or languages such as Python and R. Use ONNX Runtime to optimize and accelerate inferencing across cloud and edge devices. Track all aspects of your training experiments using MLflow.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div>

       <p>Use the central registry to store and track data, models, and metadata. Automatically capture lineage and governance data. Use Git to track work and GitHub Actions to implement workflows. Use managed endpoints to operationalize model deployment and scoring, log metrics, and perform safe model rollouts.</p>

       </svg> </span>

     <div class="column medium-5 end"> 
      <div class="row column"> 
       <h3> Responsible machine learning </h3> 
       <p>Get model transparency at training and inferencing with interpretability capabilities. Assess model fairness through disparity metrics and mitigate unfairness. Help protect data with differential privacy and confidential machine learning pipelines.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-1 text-center"> <span class="icon">

      <div class="row column"> 
       <h3> Enterprise-grade security </h3> 
       <p>Build and deploy models more securely with network isolation and private link capabilities, role-based access control for resources and actions, custom roles, and managed identity for compute resources.</p> 
      </div>

   <section id="faq" class="section" aria-label="Frequently asked questions about Azure Machine Learning" data-module="faq-01"> 
    <div class="row"> 
     <div class="column medium-3"> 
      <h2>Frequently asked questions about Azure Machine Learning</h2> 
     </div> 
     <div class="column medium-8 medium-offset-1"> 
      <ul class="faq"> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="8a8ec215" data-bi-slot="1" data-bi-id="faq-1" data-bi-an="faq-01"> Where is Azure Machine Learning available? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="8a8ec215">
         The service is <a href="/en-us/global-infrastructure/services/?products=machine-learning-service">generally available</a> in several countries/regions, with more on the way.
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="75f224f7" data-bi-slot="2" data-bi-id="faq-2" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What is the SLA? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="75f224f7">
         The <a href="/en-us/support/legal/sla/machine-learning-service/">service-level agreement</a> (SLA) for Azure Machine Learning is 99.9 percent uptime.
        </div> </li> 
       <li class="faq__item"> <button type="button" class="faq__question" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ed0531b5" data-bi-slot="3" data-bi-id="faq-3" data-bi-an="faq-01"> What is Azure Machine Learning studio? </button> 
        <div class="faq__answer" id="ed0531b5">
         Azure Machine Learning studio is the top-level resource for Machine Learning. This capability provides a centralized place for data scientists and developers to work with all the artifacts for building, training, and deploying machine learning models.
        </div> </li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
   </section>
